Path select for accel\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ACCEL\+\_\+\+FCHOICE\+\_\+\+BYPASS \+: DLPF bypassed (very wide BW, fastest)
\item ACCEL\+\_\+\+FCHOICE\+\_\+\+DLPF \+: DLPF enabled (use ACCEL\+\_\+\+DLPFCFG + SMPLRT\+\_\+\+DIV) 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item GYRO\+\_\+\+FCHOICE\+\_\+\+BYPASS \+: DLPF bypassed (widest BW, fastest)
\item GYRO\+\_\+\+FCHOICE\+\_\+\+DLPF \+: DLPF enabled (use GYRO\+\_\+\+DLPFCFG + SMPLRT\+\_\+\+DIV) 
\end{DoxyItemize}

7Semi comment style
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Full ICM-\/20948 register map (Banks 0–3) + key bit fields
\item Simple, portable \#defines for firmware use
\item Datasheet naming kept where practical; fields grouped by bank
\end{DoxyItemize}

Notes
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item WHO\+\_\+\+AM\+\_\+I expected value\+: 0x\+EA
\item Select register bank via REG\+\_\+\+BANK\+\_\+\+SEL in any bank
\item Use BANK(n) helper or write raw values 0x00/0x10/0x20/0x30
\item Identity / power / interrupts / sensor data 
\end{DoxyItemize}
